Each space in the grid contains a number. \r\nA classic Bingo game uses the numbers list starting from 1 to 75. This list displays the called out numbers. And also five columns of the card are represented by letters B, I, N, G and O from left to right. The center space is usually marked as a Free Space, and is filled already in all the cards. The range of printed numbers that can appear on the card is normally restricted by column, with the 'B' column only containing numbers between 1 and 15 inclusive, the 'I' column containing only 16 through 30, 'N' containing 31 through 45, 'G' containing 46 through 60, and 'O' containing 61 through 75.\r\nEach player try to match the numbers rolled/drawn at random with numbers on a card.
